\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
API headers and documentation for the mmg2d library. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Cecile Dobrzynski and Algiane Froehly (Bx INP/\+Inria/\+UBordeaux) 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
5 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
01 2014 
\end{DoxyDate}
\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
GNU Lesser General Public License.
\end{DoxyCopyright}
These are the API functions for the mmg2d library. These functions allow to load and save meshes and data defined on meshes; add, extract, or modify mesh data; and to call the library functions that perform meshing, remeshing, level-\/set discretization, and Lagrangian motion.

Meshes are here defined in terms of vertices and two-\/dimensional objects\+: triangles and quadrangles. Edges can also be represented. All of these {\itshape entities} can have a {\itshape reference\+:} an integer value that can serve as a group identifier. In addition mesh entities can have {\itshape attributes} such as \char`\"{}required\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}corner\char`\"{}.

Data defined on meshes can be for example functions that are meant for level-\/set discretization, metric tensors that will govern edge lengths, and vector fields governing lagrangian motion. These data can be scalar, vector, or (symmetric) tensor-\/valued; and there can be more than one data item associated with a mesh entity. These data are often referred to as {\itshape solutions}.

Four of the functions here are referred to as \char`\"{}programs\char`\"{}, because they perform the tasks for which Mmg is meant\+: (re)meshing, level-\/set discretization and Lagrangian motion. The other functions merely serve to load and save data and to perform pre-\/ and post-\/processing. These programs actually behave much like independent programs\+: they send diagnostic output to stdout and in rare cases they may call the exit() function. 

Definition in file \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmg2d_8h_source}{libmmg2d.\+h}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{libmmg2d_8h_a4d6eb9f3d94d73ae9a1429425c3a3adc}\label{libmmg2d_8h_a4d6eb9f3d94d73ae9a1429425c3a3adc}}

\index{MMG2D\_Param@{MMG2D\_Param}!libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Param}{MMG2D\_Param}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmg2d_8h_a4d6eb9f3d94d73ae9a1429425c3a3adc}{MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Param}}}



Input parameters for mmg library. 

These are the input parameters for mmg2d library functions. Options prefixed by {\itshape MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+IPARAM} require integer values and options prefixed by {\itshape MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+DPARAM} require real values. They can be set with the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__2d_8c_a3639c1a88f62b23d23203b2fbebd7a23}{MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+iparameter}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__2d_8c_ae39cf56a1e0f69f392990222a252e776}{MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+dparameter}} functions, respectively. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{MMG2D\_IPARAM\_verbose@{MMG2D\_IPARAM\_verbose}!libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}}\index{libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}!MMG2D\_IPARAM\_verbose@{MMG2D\_IPARAM\_verbose}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{libmmg2d_8h_a4d6eb9f3d94d73ae9a1429425c3a3adcad48a1f20de6a5e7c16644ff7e5031c63}\label{libmmg2d_8h_a4d6eb9f3d94d73ae9a1429425c3a3adcad48a1f20de6a5e7c16644ff7e5031c63}} 
MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+IPARAM\+\_\+verbose&\mbox{[}-\/1..10\mbox{]}, Level of verbosity \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{MMG2D\_IPARAM\_mem@{MMG2D\_IPARAM\_mem}!libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}}\index{libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}!MMG2D\_IPARAM\_mem@{MMG2D\_IPARAM\_mem}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{libmmg2d_8h_a4d6eb9f3d94d73ae9a1429425c3a3adca5d11dfdb6517f0b44078a8e7ac4b482c}\label{libmmg2d_8h_a4d6eb9f3d94d73ae9a1429425c3a3adca5d11dfdb6517f0b44078a8e7ac4b482c}}

\index{libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}!MMG2D\_Compute\_eigenv@{MMG2D\_Compute\_eigenv}}
\index{MMG2D\_Compute\_eigenv@{MMG2D\_Compute\_eigenv}!libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Compute\_eigenv()}{MMG2D\_Compute\_eigenv()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Compute\+\_\+eigenv (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{m\mbox{[}3\mbox{]},  }\item[{double}]{lambda\mbox{[}2\mbox{]},  }\item[{double}]{vp\mbox{[}2\mbox{]}\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compute the real eigenvalues and eigenvectors of a symmetric matrix. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em m} & upper part of a sym\+Metric matrix diagonalizable in $\vert$R \\
\hline
{\em lambda} & array of the metric eigenvalues \\
\hline
{\em vp} & array of the metric eigenvectors\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the order of the eigenvalues
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function computes the real eigenvalues and eigenvectors of a symmetric matrix m whose upper part is provided (m11, m12, m22, in this order).

lambda\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(1,\+:) in fortran

lambda\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}1,1\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(2,\+:) in fortran

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+COMPUTE\+\_\+\+EIGENV(m,lambda,vp,retval)~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: m($\ast$)~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: lambda($\ast$),vp($\ast$)~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

For the \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmg2d_8c_a002bd2252bae7f66816a43da71049560}{MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmg2dlib}} function, you need to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__2d_8c_a34d42982555797a0c6ba089f674279f4}{MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh}} function with the following arguments \+: MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh,  MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met,\&your\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmg2d_8c_a357e31119044dbb3e57fca56c0927abc}{MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmg2dls}} function, you need to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__2d_8c_a34d42982555797a0c6ba089f674279f4}{MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh}} function with the following arguments \+: MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls, \&your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmg2d_8c_abca343b0aa4d5a7b383c4e905a18f505}{MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmg2dmov}} function, you must call \+: MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh,  MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met,\&empty\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Disp, \&your\+\_\+displacement, \+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 on success
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
we pass the structures by reference in order to have argument compatibility between the library call from a Fortran code and a C code.

No fortran interface to allow variadic arguments.

no Fortran interface to allow variadic args. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\index{MMG2D\_Get\_edge@{MMG2D\_Get\_edge}!libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Get\_edge()}{MMG2D\_Get\_edge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Ridge,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next edge in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em e0} & pointer to the first extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em e1} & pointer to the second extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the edge reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Ridge} & pointer to the flag saying if the edge is ridge. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if the edge is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the extremities {\itshape e0}, {\itshape e1} and reference {\itshape ref} of next edge of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all edges. When it has been called as many times as there are edges in the mesh, the internal edge counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+EDGE(mesh,e0,e1,ref,is\+Ridge,is\+Required,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT)\+:: e0,e1~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Ridge,is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

Get one out of several scalar solutions at a specific vertex. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sol} & pointer to the array of solutions \\
\hline
{\em i} & position of the solution field that we want to set. \\

Get values of the ith field of the solution array at vertex {\itshape pos}. (pos from 1 to the number of vertices included and {\itshape i} from 1 to the number of solutions).

Get one out of several scalar solutions at all vertices in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em i} & position of the solution field that we want to get. \\
\hline
{\em s} & array of solutions at mesh vertices. The solution at vertex {\itshape k} is given by s\mbox{[}k-\/1\mbox{]} for a scalar sol, s\mbox{[}2$\ast$(k-\/1)\mbox{]}@2 for a vectorial solution and s\mbox{[}3$\ast$(k-\/1)\mbox{]}@3 for a tensor solution.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{MMG2D\_Get\_nonBdyEdge@{MMG2D\_Get\_nonBdyEdge}!libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Get\_nonBdyEdge()}{MMG2D\_Get\_nonBdyEdge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+non\+Bdy\+Edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{idx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get vertices and reference of a non-\/boundary edge. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em e0} & pointer to the first extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em e1} & pointer to the second extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the edge reference. \\
\hline
{\em idx} & index of the non boundary edge to get (between 1 and nb\+\_\+edges) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function returns the extremities {\itshape e0}, {\itshape e1} and reference {\itshape ref} of the idx$^\wedge$th non boundary edge (for DG methods for example). An edge is boundary if it is located at the interface of 2 domains with different references, if it belongs to one triangle only or if it is a singular edge (ridge or required).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+NONBDYEDGE(mesh,e0,e1,ref,idx,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT)\+:: e0,e1~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: idx~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\index{libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}!MMG2D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges@{MMG2D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges}}
\index{MMG2D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges@{MMG2D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges}!libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges()}{MMG2D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyEdges()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+number\+Of\+Non\+Bdy\+Edges (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{nb\+\_\+edges }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the number of non-\/boundary edges. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em nb\+\_\+edges} & pointer to the number of non boundary edges. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function extracts the number of non boundary edges (for DG methods for example). An edge is boundary if it is located at the interface of two domains with different references, if it belongs to one triangle only or if it is a singular edge (ridge or required).

Append these edges to the list of edges.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
reallocate the edge array and append the internal edges. This may modify the behaviour of other functions.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+NUMBEROFNONBDYEDGES(mesh,nb\+\_\+edges,retval)~\newline

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT)\+:: nb\+\_\+edges~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+quadrilateral (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v3,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next quadrangle of the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & pointer to the first vertex of quadrangle. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & pointer to the second vertex of quadrangle. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & pointer to the third vertex of quadrangle. \\
\hline
{\em v3} & pointer to the fourth vertex of quadrangle. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the quadrangle reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if quadrangle is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get the vertices {\itshape v0},{\itshape v1},{\itshape v2},{\itshape v3} and reference {\itshape ref} of the next quadrangle of mesh. This function is meant to be called in a loop over all quadrangles. When it has been called as many times as there are quadrangles, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Get\_triangle()}{MMG2D\_Get\_triangle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+triangle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next triangle in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & pointer to the first vertex of triangle. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & pointer to the second vertex of triangle. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & pointer to the third vertex of triangle. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the triangle reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if triangle is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1}, {\itshape v2}, and reference {\itshape ref} of the next triangle of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all triangles. When it has been called as many times as there are triangles, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TRIANGLE(mesh,v0,v1,v2,ref,is\+Required,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT)\+:: v0,v1,v2~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Get\_triFromEdge()}{MMG2D\_Get\_triFromEdge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tri\+From\+Edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ked,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ktri,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{ied }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Find a triangle given an adjacent triangle and an edge number. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em ked} & index of the boundary edge. \\
\hline
{\em ktri} & pointer to the index of the tri (filled by the function). \\
\hline
{\em ied} & pointer to the index of the edge of the triangle {\itshape ktri} that correspond to the boundary edge {\itshape ked}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Fill {\itshape ktri} by the index of the triangle to which belong a boundary edge and {\itshape ied} by the index of the edge of the triangle that correspond to the edge.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Get\_trisFromEdge()}{MMG2D\_Get\_trisFromEdge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tris\+From\+Edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ked,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ktri\mbox{[}2\mbox{]},  }\item[{int}]{ied\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Find two triangles given the edge that they share. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em ked} & index of the boundary edge. \\
\hline
{\em ktri} & pointer to an array of size 2 to fill by the indices of the triangles that share the edge {\itshape ked} (filled by the function). \\
\hline
{\em ied} & pointer to an array of size two to fill by the indices of the edge in each triangle.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Fill {\itshape ktri} by the indices of the triangles to which belong a boundary edge and {\itshape ied} by the indices of the matching edge in each triangle. If {\itshape ked} belongs to one triangle only, ktri\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} = ied\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} = 0.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval,ied~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Get\_vectorSol()}{MMG2D\_Get\_vectorSol()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+vector\+Sol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{vx,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{vy }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the next element of a vector sol structure. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em met} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em vx} & x value of the vectorial solution. \\
\hline
{\em vy} & y value of the vectorial solution. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves vectorial solution $(v_x,v_y)$ of the next element of {\itshape met}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all elements. When it has been called as many times as there are elements in the solution, the internal counter will be reset.

 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\index{MMG2D\_Get\_vertex@{MMG2D\_Get\_vertex}!libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Get\_vertex()}{MMG2D\_Get\_vertex()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+vertex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c0,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Corner,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the coordinates and reference ref of the next vertex of a mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em c0} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the first dimension. \\
\hline
{\em c1} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the second dimension. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the vertex reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Corner} & pointer to the flag saying if vertex is corner. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if vertex is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the coordinates {\itshape c0} and {\itshape c1}, and reference {\itshape ref} of the next vertex of a mesh. It is meant to be used in a loop over all vertices. When this function has been called as many times as there are vertices, the internal loop counter will be reset. To obtain data for a specific vertex, the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__2d_8c_a6626285528748ac1536a9fcfb05253da}{MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+By\+Idx\+\_\+vertex}} function can be used instead.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+VERTEX(mesh,c0,c1,ref,is\+Corner,is\+Required,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: c0,c1~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Corner,is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Init\_mesh()}{MMG2D\_Init\_mesh()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const int}]{starter,  }\item[{}]{... }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initialize a mesh structure and optionally the associated solution and metric structures. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em starter} & dummy argument used to initialize the variadic argument list \\
\hline
{\em ...} & variadic arguments.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 on success, 0 on failure
\end{DoxyReturn}
For the MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmgslib function, you need to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__2d_8c_a34d42982555797a0c6ba089f674279f4}{MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh}} function with the following arguments \+: MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met, \&your\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmgsls function, you need to call the {\itshape MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh} function with the following arguments \+: MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls, \&your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

Here, {\itshape your\+\_\+mesh} is a \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}, {\itshape your\+\_\+metric} and {\itshape your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set} are \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
No fortran interface, to allow variadic arguments. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+load\+Vtk\+Mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Load a mesh and possibly data in VTK format from file. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the metric structure or the NULL pointer. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the level-\/set structure or the NULL pointer. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & name of the file to load.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if the file is not found, -\/1 if failing for another reason (insufficient memory, file format...), 1 on success.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Read mesh and 0 or 1 data fields in VTK file format (.vtk extension). We read only low-\/order vertices, edges, triangles and quadrangles.

\hline

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_mmg2dlib()}{MMG2D\_mmg2dlib()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmg2dlib (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Main \char`\"{}program\char`\"{} for the mesh adaptation library. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to a sol structure (metric). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a4a5b6de311b295a697e73d2ba18d951f}{MMG5\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}} if successful, \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a3f7f4f4f89f2b378b6f4c91e7533f9c4}{MMG5\+\_\+\+LOWFAILURE}} in case there is a failure but a conform mesh is returned and \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a2ed44e9232d89d6464b89b86652f1090}{MMG5\+\_\+\+STRONGFAILURE}} if there is a failure and we can\textquotesingle{}t save the mesh.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function adapts a given mesh, trying to improve the quality, under the given metric and parameters.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

\end{quote}

Main \char`\"{}program\char`\"{} for the level-\/set discretization library. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to a sol structure (level-\/set function). \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to a sol structure (metric). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a4a5b6de311b295a697e73d2ba18d951f}{MMG5\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}} if successful, \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a3f7f4f4f89f2b378b6f4c91e7533f9c4}{MMG5\+\_\+\+LOWFAILURE}} if there is a failure but a conform mesh is saved and \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a2ed44e9232d89d6464b89b86652f1090}{MMG5\+\_\+\+STRONGFAILURE}} if there is a failure and we can\textquotesingle{}t save the mesh.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This is the main program for the level-\/set discretization library. If a metric {\itshape met} is provided, it is used to adapt the mesh.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+save\+Msh\+Mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Save a mesh and optionally one data field in MSH format, ascii or binary depending on the filename extension. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the solution structure. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & name of the file to write. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function writes a mesh and optionally one data field in MSH file format (.msh extension). It uses ASCII format for .msh extension, binary format for .msb extension.

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\index{libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}!MMG2D\_Set\_lsBaseReference@{MMG2D\_Set\_lsBaseReference}}
\index{MMG2D\_Set\_lsBaseReference@{MMG2D\_Set\_lsBaseReference}!libmmg2d.h@{libmmg2d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Set\_lsBaseReference()}{MMG2D\_Set\_lsBaseReference()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+ls\+Base\+Reference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{br }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set level-\/set base reference. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em br} & new level-\/set base reference. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set a new level-\/set base reference of ref {\itshape br} in ls discretization mode. Based references are boundary conditions to which implicit domain can be attached. All implicit volumes that are not attached to listed base references are deleted as spurious volumes by the {\itshape rmc} option.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN)\+:: br~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

Set the number of vertices, triangles, quadrangles and edges of the mesh and allocate the associated tables. If call twice, reset the whole mesh to realloc it at the new size

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d__export_8h_a402a2a5f04cc1a36ad12b4917e6e896e}{LIBMMG2\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+multi\+Mat (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ref,  }\item[{int}]{split,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{rmin,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{rplus }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the reference mapping for the elements of ref {\itshape ref} in LS discretization mode. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & input tetra reference. \\
\hline
{\em split} & \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_ac1d06e3937204e0222c0bbf5909f6e21}{MMG5\+\_\+\+MMAT\+\_\+\+No\+Split}} if the entity must not be split, \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a1f9cc5180d950449f7e206ffacd3f9d8}{MMG5\+\_\+\+MMAT\+\_\+\+Split}} otherwise \\
\hline
{\em rmin} & reference for the negative side after LS discretization \\
\hline
{\em rplus} & reference for the positive side after LS discretization \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on failure, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}


\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+MULTIMAT(mesh,sol,ref,split,rmin,rplus,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh,sol~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN)\+:: ref,rmin,rplus~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: split~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}
With this function you can determine which references will be given to the triangles on both sides of the level set, after discretization. Negative and positive here refer to areas where the function is smaller or larger, respectively, than the isovalue of the level set. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

Set the vertices and reference of a single triangle in a mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline

\end{DoxyReturn}
